I Love You, John
============================

|  |  |
| :--: | :-- |
| [![](../../../images/albums/8038f880ee0af158b282bcb28e37f585.jpg)<br>I Love You, John](https://emumo.xiami.com/album/443200) | **艺人**: [陈珊妮](../index.md)<br>**语种**: 国语<br>**唱片公司**: 亚神音乐, 大乐音乐<br>**发行时间**: 2011年06月17日<br>**专辑类别**: 录音室专辑<br>**专辑风格**: 独立电子乐 Indietronica, 电音流行 Electropop<br>**播放数**: 1960995<br>**收藏数**: 5306<br>**评论数**: 990<br> |

## 简介

<div>
<p class="subdown011"><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">创作女王陈珊妮</span><span style="color:#FA007A"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">词</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">/</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">曲</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">/</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">制作</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">/</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">编曲</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">/</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">演唱</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">暌违三年　全新清爽畅快大碟『</span><span lang="EN-US">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">，</span><span lang="EN-US">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">』</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">给你</span><span lang="EN-US">2011</span><span style="font-family:宋体;<br>
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">夏天的</span> <span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">城市轻电音</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">勇敢说大胆做</span><span lang="EN-US"> 6/17</span><span style="font-family:宋体;<br>
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">个性发行</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial;color:#FA007A"><span id="questionSpan">『</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">』的陈珊妮</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">让你久等了！</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">继</span><span lang="EN-US">2004</span><span style="font-family:宋体;<br>
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">年『后来我们都哭了』得到金曲奖最佳专辑制作人和最佳年度专辑的肯定；经历长达四年的漫长筹备，</span><span lang="EN-US">2008</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">年再度以『如果有一件事是重要的』一举拿下最佳国语女演唱人奖项。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">睽违两年半，陈珊妮终于推出</span><span lang="EN-US">2011</span><span style="font-family:<br>
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">全新专辑『</span><span lang="EN-US">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">，</span><span lang="EN-US">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">』。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">国语歌坛最重要的女性音乐人</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">从</span><span lang="EN-US">90</span><span style="font-family:宋体;<br>
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">年代至今，陈珊妮是国语歌坛最重要的女性音乐人之一，在这个阳盛阴衰的流行音乐环境，合作的艺人跨越地域和世代。创作林晓培的成名歌曲「烦」、制作蓝心湄最受欢迎的「你的电话」、郑秀文的电音舞曲、谢霆锋的抒情摇滚、江美琪的民谣风格，到搞怪趣味的糯米团和脱拉库；花样年华的怀旧梁朝伟、酷异独特的杨乃文、演歌双栖的影后刘若英和周迅；乃至动人疗愈的梁静茹、最受瞩目的新人</span><span lang="EN-US">Hebe...<br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">陈珊妮合作过的艺人不计其数，永远多变，永远独特。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">不只是评审老师</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">近年来，因为担任节目【超级偶像】的评审，直言不讳的个性，受到许多观众的喜爱与瞩目。其实评审工作之外，陈珊妮的幕后工作依然忙碌。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">除了音乐，她也热爱电影。</span><span lang="EN-US">2009</span><span style="font-family:<br>
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">年应侯孝贤导演的邀请，担任金马奖评审工作，而在来年首次参与电影配乐，以【艋舺】一片入围金马奖最佳电影配乐，并打败许多国家的音乐人，为台湾夺下亚太影展最佳电影音乐奖。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">期间还为包括田馥甄、梁静茹、魏如萱、张芸京、周笔畅、锺舒淇</span><span lang="EN-US">...</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">等多位歌手创作和制作，持续推出作品。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial;color:#FA007A"><span id="questionSpan">『</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">』的城市轻电音</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">陈珊妮的个人专辑，每一张都有不同的音乐风格，每一张都难以归类，多年来的累积，</span><span lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">很陈珊妮的音乐</span><span lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">俨然成为一种音乐类型。从早期新诗一般的歌词，三件式摇滚乐的曲风；到两千年之后的电子摇滚，</span><span lang="EN-US">2008</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">年的专辑更带来古典乐遇上</span><span lang="EN-US">DJ</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">的优雅电气。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
2011</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">年的全新专辑，除了全创作全制作之外，更包办了大部分的编曲工作。电子音乐不一定只能摇头，不一定风格冷冽，陈珊妮以大量取样为基底，以她最擅长的拼贴手法，创作出充满时尚都会感，节奏明快词意单纯的全新风格</span><span lang="EN-US">--“</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">城市轻电音</span><span lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">。有别以往暗黑忧伤的气氛，这张新专辑散发着爽朗愉快。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial;color:#FA007A"><span id="questionSpan">『</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">』的专辑设计</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">从第一张专辑开始，每一次都在冬天发行，向来以</span><span lang="EN-US">“</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">把黑色穿得最好看</span><span lang="EN-US">”</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">著称的陈珊妮，这次终于如愿地在她最喜欢的夏天发片，除了新专辑的曲风爽朗愉快之外，这次的新造型都是春夏的柔和明亮风格，带给大家听觉和视觉上前所未有的全新感受。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial;color:#FA007A"><span id="questionSpan">『</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">』的专辑制作</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">一个玩音乐的外国朋友突然接到母亲过世的消息。他看起来心情很平静，说这几年是他和母亲最亲近也最快乐的时光。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">当时她七十多岁时，某个平凡早晨，朋友接到母亲的电话，整个对话都是关于</span><span lang="EN-US">"</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">皇后合唱团</span><span lang="EN-US">"--</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">他们究竟是哪里来的？</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">当然那早已不是皇后合唱团活跃的年代，主唱</span><span lang="EN-US"> Freddie Mercury</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">也过世了。总之七十多岁的母亲突然变成皇后合唱团的歌迷，她想拥有所有皇后合唱团的专辑，想了解每一首歌背后的故事，想知道过去的演唱会上发生过什么。自有记忆以来从未特别喜欢过什么音乐的母亲，从此疯狂的爱上皇后合唱团，每天听的都是皇后合唱团的音乐，开始参加皇后合唱团的歌迷聚会。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">母子俩开始相约喝咖啡一起吃晚餐。</span><span lang="EN-US">"</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">你应该也跟我一样很想知道，她为什么在七十多岁的某一天迷上皇后合唱团吧！</span> <span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">于是有一天我问了，你知道她怎么说的吗？</span><span lang="EN-US">"<br><br>
<br><br>
"</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">我从电台听到他们的歌</span><span lang="EN-US">..</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">你不觉得皇后合唱团很棒吗？</span><span lang="EN-US">"<br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">这是一个直率又自然的理由，只是我们都没想到而已。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">他说母亲的晚年过得很开心，因为皇后合唱团的音乐，因为开始对他的工作感兴趣，因为那些愉快的电话和约会。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">我们是从几岁开始不再关心流行音乐呢？几岁开始不再参加摇滚演唱会？什么时候开始讨厌年轻人的装扮和语汇？却又希望自己看起来仍然像个年轻人。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">什么时候开始开欧巴桑的玩笑？用那种类似欧巴桑的口气</span><span lang="EN-US">...<br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">我们可以像个大人，起床时接受镜子里自己的样子，睡前反省自己的人生。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">我们也可以像个孩子，无时无刻想些有趣的事，累积种种聊赖的梦想。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">我们可以很热血，可以很忧伤，也可以很摆烂，我们可以更成熟同时充满青春的幻想。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">这是一张这样的专辑</span><span lang="EN-US">-- </span><span style="font-family:<br>
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">就像成长从来不是什么秘密，面对未来全凭揣测，我们只需尽量变成比想象中更好的人。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial;color:#FA007A"><span id="questionSpan">『</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#FA007A">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;color:#FA007A">』的歌曲介绍</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">网络预购强打「青春」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">音乐记忆了关于青春的种种美好，我们藉由对音乐的热情，继续对青春的向往。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">首波主打「</span><span lang="EN-US">I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">，</span><span lang="EN-US">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">这首歌</span><span lang="EN-US">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体;<br>
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">要献给这个世代的可爱美眉。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">灵感来自宅神朱学恒某日噗浪写了</span><span lang="EN-US">: </span><span style="font-family:<br>
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">学习正妹网络语言中</span><span lang="EN-US">:"</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:<br>
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">干嘛</span><span lang="EN-US">John!"<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">美眉们惯用的可爱语气，竟然变成了一首歌</span><span lang="EN-US">...<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">年轻人都很爱</span><span lang="EN-US">John</span><span style="font-family:宋体;<br>
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">，所以</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
I Love You</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">，</span><span lang="EN-US">John.<br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">第二主打「双人体操」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">灵感来自国民健康操。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">良好的人际关系，需要更多快乐的肢体互动。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">网友竞相推荐「</span><span lang="EN-US">OK</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">随着年龄和成长，生活上有越来越多不如预期的事，我们会需要一些自我安慰，或许告诉自己还</span><span lang="EN-US">OK</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">，心情就会随着好转。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">「</span><span lang="EN-US">B</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">级动作片」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">层出不穷的罢凌事件，新闻中的家庭悲剧不停上演，很多时候，我们不须要使用那么多暴力来解决生活上的所有问题。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">「</span><span lang="EN-US">Naive</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">或许大家都觉得我是个聪明早慧的人，我却经常看到自己天真任性的一面，也说不定每个大人都有一颗想耍无赖的心</span><span lang="EN-US">...<br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">「晚安曲」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">我们都希望给自己挚爱的人满满的爱，希望他每天一夜好眠，希望有一首只为他准备的「晚安曲」</span><span lang="EN-US">...<br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">「美好人生」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">如果人生是一首歌，我们期待它的副歌是什么样的呢</span><span lang="EN-US">?<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">要够流行容易传唱又好记，还是只留给知心的人反复聆听</span><span lang="EN-US">...<br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">「</span><span lang="EN-US">Bitte</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;<br>
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">想写一首歌关于现在女性对爱的渴望，很多女人等爱等的痛苦，处心积虑的想找到那种被爱的感觉，却忘了倾听自己的心，先接受对自己的爱。</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
<br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体">★</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial">「爱情」</span><span lang="EN-US"><br><br>
</span><span style="font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:<br>
Arial">真正爱一个人的时候，你只想留给他最快乐的时间，最好的消息，和他分享生命中最美好的一切</span><span lang="EN-US">... <o:p></o:p></span></p><br>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
</div>
